		<div class="entry-content" itemprop="text">

<div><div class="gb-looper-6b5413d4">

<a href="https://yumvet.com/sweet-and-savory-pineapple-chicken-and-rice-recipe/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img data-perfmatters-preload fetchpriority="high" decoding="async" width="960" height="1200" data-media-id="7631" class="gb-media-6a46e7a2" src="https://yumvet.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/01/5.-Sweet-and-Savory-Pineapple-Chicken-and-Rice-Recipe-1.webp" alt="Sweet and Savory Pineapple Chicken and Rice Recipe" srcset="https://yumvet.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/01/5.-Sweet-and-Savory-Pineapple-Chicken-and-Rice-Recipe-1.webp 960w, https://yumvet.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/01/5.-Sweet-and-Savory-Pineapple-Chicken-and-Rice-Recipe-1-240x300.webp 240w, https://yumvet.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/01/5.-Sweet-and-Savory-Pineapple-Chicken-and-Rice-Recipe-1-819x1024.webp 819w, https://yumvet.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/01/5.-Sweet-and-Savory-Pineapple-Chicken-and-Rice-Recipe-1-768x960.webp 768w" sizes="(max-width: 960px) 100vw, 960px" title="Home Page 1" loading="eager"></a>



<h2 class="gb-text gb-text-2742e2dd"><a href="https://yumvet.com/sweet-and-savory-pineapple-chicken-and-rice-recipe/">Sweet and Savory Pineapple Chicken and Rice Recipe</a></h2>

<p>Hi, I’m Lila. I’m so happy you’re here.</p>



<p>YumVet began most simply, on a quiet Sunday afternoon in my small kitchen. My friends Naomi and Emery were there, helping me test a new recipe as we chatted about everything and nothing at all. Amid the laughter, the inevitable mess, and the warm aroma of something baking, it clicked. Those ordinary moments, cooking, organizing, styling, and creating side by side, were exactly where our joy lived.</p>
